type=\"text/javascript\">\n    $(document).ready(function() {\n        channelHoverIE();\n        channelTouch();\n        closeMenuByPressingKey();\n    });\n\n    function channelTouch() {\n        // this will change the dropdown behavior when it is touched vs clicked.\n        // channels will be clickable on second click. first click simply opens the menu.\n        $('#channel-navigation > .sw-channel-item > a').on({\n            'touchstart': function (e) {\n                \n                // see if has menu\n                if ($(this).siblings('ul.sw-channel-dropdown li').length > 0) {\n                    var button = $(this);\n\n                    // add href as property if not already set\n                    // then remove href attribute\n                    if (!button.prop('linkHref')) {\n                        button.prop('linkHref', button.attr('href'));\n                        button.removeAttr('href');\n                    }\n\n                    // check to see if menu is already open\n                    if ($(this).siblings('ul.sw-channel-dropdown').is(':visible')) {\n                        // if open go to link\n                        window.location.href = button.prop('linkHref');\n                    } \n\n                } \n            }\n        });\n    }\n\n\n    \n    function channelHoverIE(){\n\t\t// set z-index for IE7\n\t\tvar parentZindex = $('#channel-navigation').parents('div:first').css('z-index');\n\t\tvar zindex = (parentZindex > 0 ? parentZindex : 8000);\n\t\t$(\".sw-channel-item\").each(function(ind) {\n\t\t\t$(this).css('z-index', zindex - ind);\n\t\t\tzindex --;\n\t\t});\n\t    $(\".sw-channel-item\").hover(function(){\n\t        var subList = $(this).children('ul');\n\t        if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== \"\") {\n\t            subList.show();\n\t            subList.attr(\"aria-hidden\", \"false\");\n\t\t    }\n\t\t    $(this).addClass(\"hover\");\n\t    }, function() {\n\t        $(\".sw-channel-dropdown\").hide();\n\t        $(this).removeClass(\"hover\");\n\t        var subList = $(this).children('ul');\n\t        if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== \"\") {\n\t            subList.attr(\"aria-hidden\", \"true\");\n\t        }\n\t    });\n    }\n\n    function closeMenuByPressingKey() {\n        $(\".sw-channel-item\").each(function(ind) {\n            $(this).keyup(function (event) {\n                if (event.keyCode == 27) { // ESC\n                    $(\".sw-channel-dropdown\").hide();\n                    $(this).removeClass(\"hover\");\n                    var subList = $(this).children('ul');\n                    if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== \"\") {\n                        subList.attr(\"aria-hidden\", \"true\");\n                    }\n                    $(this).next().find('a:first').focus();\n                }\n            });\n        });\n\n        $(\".sw-channel-dropdown li\").each(function(ind) {\n            $(this).keyup(function (event) {\n                if (event.keyCode == 9) { // TAB\n                    $(\".sw-channel-dropdown\").hide();\n                    var parentMenuItem = $(this).parent().closest('li');\n                    parentMenuItem.removeClass(\"hover\");\n                    var subList = parentMenuItem.children('ul');\n                    if ($.trim(subList.html()) !== \"\") {\n                        subList.attr(\"aria-hidden\", \"true\");\n                    }\n                    parentMenuItem.next().find('a:first').focus();\n                }\n            });\n        });\n    }\n\n</script>\n\n\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</div>\n        <div id=\"hp-slideshow\" class=\"hide480\" style=\"height: 400.51px;\">\n\t\t\t<a   appStoreLanguage: 'us', // Language code for App Store\n                    inAppStore: 'On the App Store', // Text after price for iOS\n                    inGooglePlay: 'In Google Play', // Text after price for Android\n                    inAmazonAppStore: 'In the Amazon Appstore',\n                    inWindowsStore: 'In the Windows Store', //Text of price for Windows\n                    GooglePlayParams: null, // Aditional parameters for the market\n                    icon: 'GlobalAssets/Images/MobileNative/sw_app_logo.png', // The URL of the icon - SET THIS TO THE iOS APP STORE ICON \n\t\t\t    iconGloss: false, // Force gloss effect\n\t\t\t    button: 'VIEW', // Text for the install button\n\t\t\t    url: null, // The URL for the button. Keep null if you want the button to link to the app store.\n\t\t\t    scale: 'auto', // Scale based on viewport size (set to 1 to disable)\n\t\t\t    speedIn: 300, // Show animation speed of the banner\n\t\t\t    speedOut: 400, // Close animation speed of the banner\n\t\t\t    daysHidden: 1, // Duration to hide the banner after being closed (0 = always show banner)\n\t\t\t    daysReminder: 30, // Duration to hide the banner after \"VIEW\" is clicked *separate from when the close button is clicked* (0 = always show banner)\n\t\t\t    force: null, // Choose 'ios' or 'android'. Don't do a browser check, just always show this banner\n\t\t\t    hideOnInstall: true, // Hide the banner after \"VIEW\" is clicked.\n\t\t\t    layer: false, // Display as overlay layer or slide down the page\n\t\t\t    iOSUniversalApp: true, // If the iOS App is a universal app for both iPad and iPhone, display Smart Banner to iPad users, too.\n\t\t\t    appendToSelector: 'body', //Append the banner to a specific selector\n\t\t\t    pushSelector: 'html' // What element is going to push the site content down; this is where the banner append animation will start.\n                });\n            });\n\n        // DO NOT EDIT BELOW THIS LINE\n\n        /*!\n * jQuery Smart Banner\n * Copyright (c) 2012 Arnold Daniels <arnold@jasny.net>\n * Based on 'jQuery Smart Web App Banner' by Kurt Zenisek @ kzeni.com\n */\n        !function ($) {\n            var SmartBanner = function (options) {\n                this.origHtmlMargin = parseFloat($('html').css('margin-top')) // Get the original margin-top of the HTML element so we can take that into account\n                this.options = $.extend({}, $.smartbanner.defaults, options)\n\n                var standalone = navigator.standalone // Check if it's already a standalone web app or running within a webui view of an app (not mobile safari)\n                  , UA = navigator.userAgent\n\n                // Detect banner type (iOS or Android)\n                if (this.options.force) {\n                    this.type = this.options.force\n                } else if (UA.match(/Windows Phone 8/i) != null && UA.match(/Touch/i) !== null) {\n                    this.type = 'windows'\n                } else if (UA.match(/iPhone|iPod/i) != null || (UA.match(/iPad/) && this.options.iOSUniversalApp)) {\n                    if (UA.match(/Safari/i) != null &&\n                       (UA.match(/CriOS/i) != null ||\n                       window.Number(UA.substr(UA.indexOf('OS ') + 3, 3).replace('_', '.')) < 6)) this.type = 'ios' // Check webview and native smart banner support (iOS 6+)\n                } else if (UA.match(/\\bSilk\\/(.*\\bMobile Safari\\b)?/) || UA.match(/\\bKF\\w/) || UA.match('Kindle Fire')) {\n                    this.type = 'kindle'\n                } else if (UA.match(/Android/i) != null) {\n                    this.type = 'android'\n                }\n\n                // Don't show banner if device isn't iOS or Android, website is loaded in app or user dismissed banner\n                if (!this.type || standalone || this.getCookie('sb-closed') || this.getCookie('sb-installed')) {\n                    return\n                }\n\n                // Calculate scale\n                this.scale = this.options.scale == 'auto' ? $(window).width() / window.screen.width : this.options.scale\n                if (this.scale < 1) this.scale = 1\n\n                // Get info from meta data\n                var meta = $(this.type == 'android' ? 'meta[name=\"google-play-app\"]' :\n                    this.type == 'ios' ? 'meta[name=\"apple-itunes-app\"]' :\n                    this.type == 'kindle' ? 'meta[name=\"kindle-fire-app\"]' : 'meta[name=\"msApplication-ID\"]');\n                if (meta.length == 0) return\n\n                // For Windows Store apps, get the PackageFamilyName for protocol launch\n                if (this.type == 'windows') {\n                    this.appId = $('meta[name=\"msApplication-PackageFamilyName\"]').attr('content');\n                } else {\n                    // Try to pull the appId out of the meta tag and store the result\n                    var parsedMetaContent = /app-id=([^\\s,]+)/.exec(meta.attr('content'));\n\n                    if (parsedMetaContent) {\n                        this.appId = parsedMetaContent[1];\n                    } else {\n                        return;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                this.title = this.options.title ? this.options.title : meta.data('title') || $('title').text().replace(/\\s*[|\\-·].*$/, '')\n                this.author = this.options.author ? this.options.author : meta.data('author') || ($('meta[name=\"author\"]').length ? $('meta[name=\"author\"]').attr('content') : window.location.hostname)\n                this.iconUrl = meta.data('icon-url');\n                this.price = meta.data('price');\n\n                // Create banner\n                this.create()\n                this.show()\n                this.listen()\n            }\n\n            SmartBanner.prototype = {\n\n                constructor: SmartBanner\n\n              , create: function () {\n                  var iconURL\n                    , link = (this.options.url ? this.options.url : (this.type == 'windows' ? 'ms-windows-store:navigate?appid=' : (this.type == 'android' ? 'market://details?id=' : (this.type == 'kindle' ? 'amzn://apps/android?asin=' : 'https://itunes.apple.com/' + this.options.appStoreLanguage + '/app/id'))) + this.appId)\n                    , price = this.price || this.options.price\n                    , inStore = price ? price + ' - ' + (this.type == 'android' ? this.options.inGooglePlay : this.type == 'kindle' ? this.options.inAmazonAppStore : this.type == 'ios' ? this.options.inAppStore : this.options.inWindowsStore) : ''\n                    , gloss = this.options.iconGloss === null ? (this.type == 'ios') : this.options.iconGloss\n\n                  if (this.type == 'android' && this.options.GooglePlayParams) {\n                      link = link + '&referrer=' + this.options.GooglePlayParams;\n                  }\n\n                  var banner = '<div id=\"smartbanner\" class=\"' + this.type + '\"><div class=\"sb-container\"><a href=\"#\" class=\"sb-close\">&times;</a><span class=\"sb-icon\"></span><div class=\"sb-info\"><strong>' + this.title + '</strong><span>' + this.author + '</span><span>' + inStore + '</span></div><a href=\"' + link + '\" class=\"sb-button\"><span>' + this.options.button + '</span></a></div></div>';\n                  (this.options.layer) ? $(this.options.appendToSelector).append(banner) : $(this.options.appendToSelector).prepend(banner);\n\n                  if (this.options.icon) {\n                      iconURL = this.options.icon\n                  } else if (this.iconUrl) {\n                      iconURL = this.iconUrl;\n                  } else if ($('link[rel=\"apple-touch-icon-precomposed\"]').length > 0) {\n                      iconURL = $('link[rel=\"apple-touch-icon-precomposed\"]').attr('href')\n                      if (this.options.iconGloss === null) gloss = false\n                  } else if ($('link[rel=\"apple-touch-icon\"]').length > 0) {\n                      iconURL = $('link[rel=\"apple-touch-icon\"]').attr('href')\n                  } else if ($('meta[name=\"msApplication-TileImage\"]').length > 0) {\n                      iconURL = $('meta[name=\"msApplication-TileImage\"]').attr('content')\n                  } else if ($('meta[name=\"msapplication-TileImage\"]').length > 0) { /* redundant because ms docs show two case usages */\n                      iconURL = $('meta[name=\"msapplication-TileImage\"]').attr('content')\n                  }\n\n                  if (iconURL) {\n                      $('#smartbanner .sb-icon').css('background-image', 'url(' + iconURL + ')')\n                      if (gloss) $('#smartbanner .sb-icon').addClass('gloss')\n                  } else {\n                      $('#smartbanner').addClass('no-icon')\n                  }\n\n                  this.bannerHeight = $('#smartbanner').outerHeight() + 2\n\n                  if (this.scale > 1) {\n                      $('#smartbanner')\n                          .css('top', parseFloat($('#smartbanner').css('top')) * this.scale)\n                          .css('height', parseFloat($('#smartbanner').css('height')) * this.scale)\n                          .hide()\n                      $('#smartbanner .sb-container')\n                          .css('-webkit-transform', 'scale(' + this.scale + ')')\n                          .css('-msie-transform', 'scale(' + this.scale + ')')\n                          .css('-moz-transform', 'scale(' + this.scale + ')')\n                          .css('width', $(window).width() / this.scale)\n                  }\n                  if(this.options.layer==false){\n                      $('#smartbanner').css('position', 'static');\n                      if (this.type == 'android') {\n                          $('#smartbanner').css({'position':'relative','top':'0px','left':'0px'});\n                      }\n                  }else{\n                      $('#smartbanner').css('position', 'absolute');\n                  }\n              }\n\n              , listen: function () {\n                  $('#smartbanner .sb-close').on('click', $.proxy(this.close, this))\n                  $('#smartbanner .sb-button').on('click', $.proxy(this.install, this))\n              }\n\n              , show: function (callback) {\n                  var banner = $('#smartbanner');\n                  banner.stop();\n\n                  if (this.options.layer) {\n                      banner.animate({ top: 0, display: 'block' }, this.options.speedIn).addClass('shown').show();\n                      $(this.pushSelector).animate({ paddingTop: this.origHtmlMargin + (this.bannerHeight * this.scale) }, this.options.speedIn, 'swing', callback);\n                  } else {\n                      if ($.support.transition) {\n                          banner.animate({ top: 0 }, this.options.speedIn).addClass('shown');\n                          var transitionCallback = function () {\n                              $('html').removeClass('sb-animation');\n                              if (callback) {\n                                  callback();\n                              }\n                          };\n                          $(this.pushSelector).addClass('sb-animation').one($.support.transition.end, transitionCallback).emulateTransitionEnd(this.options.speedIn).css('margin-top', this.origHtmlMargin + (this.bannerHeight * this.scale));\n                      } else {\n                          banner.slideDown(this.options.speedIn).addClass('shown');\n                      }\n                  }\n              }\n\n              , hide: function (callback) {\n                  var banner = $('#smartbanner');\n                  banner.stop();\n\n                  if (this.options.layer) {\n                      banner.animate({ top: -1 * this.bannerHeight * this.scale, display: 'block' }, this.options.speedIn).removeClass('shown');\n                      $(this.pushSelector).animate({ paddingTop: this.origHtmlMargin }, this.options.speedIn, 'swing', callback);\n                  } else {\n                      if ($.support.transition) {\n                          if (this.type !== 'android')\n                              banner.css('top', -1 * this.bannerHeight * this.scale).removeClass('shown');\n                          else\n                              banner.css({ display: 'none' }).removeClass('shown');\n                          var transitionCallback = function () {\n                              $('html').removeClass('sb-animation');\n                              if (callback) {\n                                  callback();\n                              }\n                          };\n                          $(this.pushSelector).addClass('sb-animation').one($.support.transition.end, transitionCallback).emulateTransitionEnd(this.options.speedOut).css('margin-top', this.origHtmlMargin);\n                      } else {\n                          banner.slideUp(this.options.speedOut).removeClass('shown');\n                      }\n                  }\n              }\n\n              , close: function (e) {\n                  e.preventDefault()\n                  this.hide()\n                  this.setCookie('sb-closed', 'true', this.options.daysHidden);\n              }\n\n              , install: function (e) {\n                  if (this.options.hideOnInstall) {\n                      this.hide()\n                  }\n                  this.setCookie('sb-installed', 'true', this.options.daysReminder)\n              }\n\n              , setCookie: function (name, value, exdays) {\n                  var exdate = new Date()\n                  exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays)\n                  value = encodeURI(value) + ((exdays == null) ? '' : '; expires=' + exdate.toUTCString())\n                  document.cookie = name + '=' + value + '; path=/;'\n              }\n\n              , getCookie: function (name) {\n                  var i, x, y, ARRcookies = document.cookie.split(\";\")\n                  for (i = 0; i < ARRcookies.length; i++) {\n                      x = ARRcookies[i].substr(0, ARRcookies[i].indexOf(\"=\"))\n                      y = ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf(\"=\") + 1)\n                      x = x.replace(/^\\s+|\\s+$/g, \"\")\n                      if (x == name) {\n                          return decodeURI(y)\n                      }\n                  }\n                  return null\n              }\n\n                // Demo only\n              , switchType: function () {\n                  var that = this\n\n                  this.hide(function () {\n                      that.type = that.type == 'android' ? 'ios' : 'android'\n                      var meta = $(that.type == 'android' ? 'meta[name=\"google-play-app\"]' : 'meta[name=\"apple-itunes-app\"]').attr('content')\n                      that.appId = /app-id=([^\\s,]+)/.exec(meta)[1]\n\n                      $('#smartbanner').detach()\n                      that.create()\n                      that.show()\n                  })\n              }\n            }\n\n            $.smartbanner = function (option) {\n                var $window = $(window)\n                , data = $window.data('smartbanner')\n                , options = typeof option == 'object' && option\n                if (!data) $window.data('smartbanner', (data = new SmartBanner(options)))\n                if (typeof option == 'string') data[option]()\n            }\n\n            // override these globally if you like (they are all optional)\n            $.smartbanner.defaults = {\n                title: null, // What the title of the app should be in the banner (defaults to <title>)\n                author: null, // What the author of the app should be in the banner (defaults to <meta name=\"author\"> or hostname)\n                price: 'FREE', // Price of the app\n                appStoreLanguage: 'us', // Language code for App Store\n                inAppStore: 'On the App Store', // Text of price for iOS\n                inGooglePlay: 'In Google Play', // Text of price for Android\n                inAmazonAppStore: 'In the Amazon Appstore',\n                inWindowsStore: 'In the Windows Store', //Text of price for Windows\n                GooglePlayParams: null, // Aditional parameters for the market\n                icon: null, // The URL of the icon (defaults to <meta name=\"apple-touch-icon\">)\n                iconGloss: null, // Force gloss effect for iOS even for precomposed\n                button: 'VIEW', // Text for the install button\n                url: null, // The URL for the button. Keep null if you want the button to link to the app store.\n                scale: 'auto', // Scale based on viewport size (set to 1 to disable)\n                speedIn: 300, // Show animation speed of the banner\n                speedOut: 400, // Close animation speed of the banner\n                daysHidden: 15, // Duration to hide the banner after being closed (0 = always show banner)\n                daysReminder: 90, // Duration to hide the banner after \"VIEW\" is clicked *separate from when the close button is clicked* (0 = always show banner)\n                force: null, // Choose 'ios', 'android' or 'windows'. Don't do a browser check, just always show this banner\n                hideOnInstall: true, // Hide the banner after \"VIEW\" is clicked.\n                layer: false, // Display as overlay layer or slide down the page\n                iOSUniversalApp: true, // If the iOS App is a universal app for both iPad and iPhone, display Smart Banner to iPad users, too.\n                appendToSelector: 'body', //Append the banner to a specific selector\n                pushSelector: 'html' // What element is going to push the site content down; this is where the banner append animation will start.\n            }\n\n            $.smartbanner.Constructor = SmartBanner;\n\n\n            // ============================================================\n            // Bootstrap transition\n            // Copyright 2011-2014 Twitter, Inc.\n            // Licensed under MIT (https://github.com/twbs/bootstrap/blob/master/LICENSE)\n\n            function transitionEnd() {\n                var el = document.createElement('smartbanner')\n\n                var transEndEventNames = {\n                    WebkitTransition: 'webkitTransitionEnd',\n                    MozTransition: 'transitionend',\n                    OTransition: 'oTransitionEnd otransitionend',\n                    transition: 'transitionend'\n                }\n\n                for (var name in transEndEventNames) {\n                    if (el.style[name] !== undefined) {\n                        return { end: transEndEventNames[name] }\n                    }\n                }\n\n                return false // explicit for ie8 (  ._.)\n            }\n\n            if ($.support.transition !== undefined)\n                return  // Prevent conflict with Twitter Bootstrap\n\n            // http://blog.alexmaccaw.com/css-transitions\n            $.fn.emulateTransitionEnd = function (duration) {\n                var called = false, $el = this\n                $(this).one($.support.transition.end, function () {\n                    called = true\n                })\n                var callback = function () {\n                    if (!called) $($el).trigger($.support.transition.end)\n                }\n                setTimeout(callback, duration)\n                return this\n            }\n\n            $(function () {\n                $.support.transition = transitionEnd()\n            })\n            // ============================================================\n\n        }(window.jQuery);\n\n        </script>\n\n        <!-- \n
